name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Friends
info:7 Reviews
rating:3.3
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Let's talk about the advantages first:
1. It is far from all scenic spots, the hotel environment is very good, and 80% of the room fee should be given to the hotel environment. It is suitable for more than 4 people to stay in the hotel and enjoy the vacation. It has its own tea room, children's playground, etc. The environment can be given 5 stars;
2. There are not as many insects as said on the Internet, maybe because it is not summer yet;
Let's talk about the disadvantages:
1. The house type problem. The two rooms booked are both on the second floor, and they are also Yinxi house types. The first floor has its own independent canopy and yard, and there is a place to sit outdoors, which is a bad review;
2. Odor problem. There is a sewer odor in the bathroom;
3. TV projection. Because the hotel has unified Wi-Fi, the TV is often projected from other rooms, and there is no solution when asking the front desk;
4. Hotel meals. The breakfast is remarkable, but the dinner for 4 people is more than 500 yuan, and it is estimated that they are all pre-prepared dishes after being served. Due to the remote location, there are few takeaway options. (I can accept the remote location and high dining costs, but at least the food should not be warm when it is served. This dinner would probably cost less than 100 yuan outside)
5. Hotel service. The hotel was cleaned in the morning, but in the afternoon, there were still waiters who did not knock on the door (at least we did not hear it) and pushed the door open directly.
In general, the environment was far beyond expectations and very comfortable, but the room, service and dining did not meet the standards of similar hotels.

msg:The hotel has a total of 60 rooms, which are not bad, but the facilities are not up to par with the hotel pricing.
There is only one restaurant in the entire area, and there are no other dining options. If you want to go somewhere else, you need to drive a mountain road, which is not convenient. The restaurant service experience is very poor. I stayed during the Chinese New Year. There were three waiters during dinner. Some dishes on the menu were not available during the Chinese New Year. The rice was not served after the dishes were finished. In addition, the dishes were almost cold when they were served, and they were particularly unpalatable! It was not until we checked out that we found out that we had missed a dish.
Let's talk about breakfast. After entering, we were asked to report the room number. The way we reported was slightly different from the record, but it did not affect the understanding of the staff. However, the other party told us that our room was not on the list and said that it was not his problem. There was no attitude to help guests solve the problem. Later, I asked the housekeeper to solve the problem. The bar is at the entrance of the restaurant. Everyone is accustomed to using the plates under the bar to serve food. The waiters reminded the guests one by one to put down the tableware in their hands and take the tableware on each table, which is very unreasonable. There are no hot food options such as soup noodles and wontons for breakfast, and the taste is not commented on. I don't know if it was because of the shortage of chefs and waiters during the Chinese New Year. In addition, the waiter stood with the dining list and watched everyone take the food. He asked us which room we were in several times. Did the hotel have the most basic employee training? The experience was very poor.
Another reason for choosing this hotel this time is because it is pet-friendly. The cleaning fee is 500/night, but the hotel does not provide any dog â€‹â€‹supplies, including tableware and dog beds. In fact, many puppies do not need additional cleaning work. I wonder if such a charging standard is reasonable?
Design alone without later supporting facilities, operations, etc. is not an excellent vacation choice. You can choose other places to spend in Anji. The above is for reference only.

posted:Posted February 5, 2024
msg:As one of the few village-style luxury resort hotels in China, this place is very different from ordinary B&Bs.

The parking lot is spacious. Walk into the hotel, cross the small bridge, and the lobby is right in front of you.
It took a while to walk around. It consists of 12 small courtyards, each with its own characteristics, independent and private.
It is especially suitable for several families to come together to rent a building, friends to get together, and company team building.

The public area's swimming pool, bar, restaurant, hot spring pool and other areas are very well designed, overlapping with bamboo forests and mountains.
What surprised me most was the hotel's children's playground, which is double-decker. Although it is not big, it is friendly enough for young children.

If you only stay in one room, the first choice is the pool room. I really recommend it!
You can see the waterfront platform, swimming pool and mountain view from the room.

msg:I came from Anji Indigo. I drove the mountain road for a long time. In fact, I was a little nervous, but when I arrived, I found that I didnâ€™t drive for so long. The hotel is surrounded by mountains, and the mountains are covered with bamboo forests. From the room, you can see the mountains around , You can still see snow-capped mountains in winter, which is better than Indigo, because Indigo is less able to see such beautiful mountain scenery. Besides the service, the butler Da Qiao is also very considerate, trying his best to meet the requirements of the guests, even if there is a small problem, he even sent a special cocktail. The room is very Nordic style, the mini bar is very sincere, the noodles and quicksand croissants for breakfast are also delicious, and I even gave a souvenir when I left. It's a pity that you can't use the beautiful swimming pool in winter, and the water temperature in the room is sometimes not hot enough. Another point is that you must go on a sunny day. The sky is blue and the mountains are emerald. If it is cloudy and the Nordic style The building will be dusty, and the experience will be much worse.

msg:Environment: The first few pictures were taken on a cloudy day on Saturday, and the following pictures were taken on a sunny day on Sunday. I have stayed in several hotels of the same price range in Anji. To be honest, the environment really does not meet the pricing and is a bit too rural. . .

Facilities: No facilities at all. As a high-end priced hotel, there are no hooks in the bathroom and the non-slip mats are not placed nearby. I personally think these mistakes should not be made.

Service: I asked for a replacement latex pillow before going to bed, and it took more than half an hour to find it before delivering it to the room. . . p.s. Butler Xiaoqiâ€™s service was ok, and she sent coffee without having afternoon tea.

Summary: Not worth the price of admission
